```r
counters <- lapply(df, table)

for (i in 1:length(counters)) {
  if (names(counters)[i] == "Central.Air") {
     column <- names(counters)[i]
    print(paste("Kolumna:", column))
    print(counters[[i]])
    print("---------------------------") 
  }
}
```

<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->


<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxubGlicmFyeShjbGFzcylcbnRyYWluX3NldCA8LSBkZlt0cmFpbiwgYyhcIk92ZXJhbGwuUXVhbFwiLCBcIlBhdmVkLkRyaXZlXCIpXVxudGVzdF9zZXQgPC0gZGZbIXRyYWluLCBjKFwiT3ZlcmFsbC5RdWFsXCIsIFwiUGF2ZWQuRHJpdmVcIildXG5DZW50cmFsLkFpclRfdHJhaW4gPC0gZGYkQ2VudHJhbC5BaXJUW3RyYWluXVxuYWlyX2tubl8xIDwtIGtubih0cmFpbl9zZXQsIHRlc3Rfc2V0LCBDZW50cmFsLkFpclRfdHJhaW4sIGsgPSAxKVxuYGBgIn0= -->

```r
library(class)
train_set <- df[train, c("Overall.Qual", "Paved.Drive")]
test_set <- df[!train, c("Overall.Qual", "Paved.Drive")]
Central.AirT_train <- df$Central.AirT[train]
air_knn_1 <- knn(train_set, test_set, Central.AirT_train, k = 1)
```

<!-- rnb-source-end -->

<!-- rnb-output-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiT3N0cnplxbxlbmllOiBwb2phd2nFgnkgc2nEmSB3YXJ0b8WbY2kgTkEgbmEgc2t1dGVrIHByemVrc3p0YcWCY2VuaWFPc3RyemXFvGVuaWU6IHBvamF3acWCeSBzacSZIHdhcnRvxZtjaSBOQSBuYSBza3V0ZWsgcHJ6ZWtzenRhxYJjZW5pYULFgsSFZCB3IHBvbGVjZW5pdSAna25uKHRyYWluX3NldCwgdGVzdF9zZXQsIENlbnRyYWwuQWlyVF90cmFpbiwgayA9IDEpJzpcbiAgd2FydG/Fm8SHIE5BL05hTi9JbmYgdyB3eXdvxYJhbml1IG9iY2VqIGZ1bmNqaSAoYXJndW1lbnQgNilcbiJ9 -->

Walidacja krzyowa:


<!-- rnb-text-end -->


<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->


<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxuc2V0LnNlZWQoMSlcbm4gPC0gbnJvdyhkZilcbnRyYWluIDwtIHNhbXBsZShuLCBuIC8gMilcbmBgYCJ9 -->

```r
set.seed(1)
n <- nrow(df)
train <- sample(n, n / 2)
```

<!-- rnb-source-end -->

<!-- rnb-chunk-end -->


<!-- rnb-text-begin -->




<!-- rnb-text-end -->


<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->


<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxuZGZfbG0gPC0gbG0oU2FsZVByaWNlIH4gT3ZlcmFsbC5RdWFsLCBkYXRhID0gZGYsIHN1YnNldCA9IHRyYWluKVxudmFsaWRhdGlvbl9zZXQgPC0gZGZbLXRyYWluLF1cbm1zZSA8LSBtZWFuKCh2YWxpZGF0aW9uX3NldCRTYWxlUHJpY2UgLSBwcmVkaWN0KGRmX2xtLCB2YWxpZGF0aW9uX3NldCkpXjIpXG5tc2VcbmBgYCJ9 -->

```r
df_lm <- lm(SalePrice ~ Overall.Qual, data = df, subset = train)
validation_set <- df[-train,]
mse <- mean((validation_set$SalePrice - predict(df_lm, validation_set))^2)
mse
```

```r
for (i in 2:5) {
  df_lm_poly <- lm(SalePrice ~ poly(Overall.Qual, degree = i), data = df, 
                     subset = train)
  print(mean((validation_set$SalePrice - predict(df_lm_poly, validation_set))^2))
}
```

<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxuc2V0LnNlZWQoMylcbnRyYWluIDwtIHNhbXBsZShuLCBuIC8gMilcbnZhbGlkYXRpb25fc2V0IDwtIGRmWy10cmFpbixdXG5kZWdyZWVfbWF4IDwtIDVcbm1zZSA8LSByZXAoMCwgdGltZXMgPSBkZWdyZWVfbWF4KVxuZm9yIChpIGluIDE6ZGVncmVlX21heCkge1xuICBkZl9sbSA8LSBsbShTYWxlUHJpY2UgfiBwb2x5KE92ZXJhbGwuUXVhbCwgZGVncmVlID0gaSksIGRhdGEgPSBkZiwgc3Vic2V0ID0gdHJhaW4pXG4gIG1zZVtpXSA8LSBtZWFuKCh2YWxpZGF0aW9uX3NldCRTYWxlUHJpY2UgLSBwcmVkaWN0KGRmX2xtLCB2YWxpZGF0aW9uX3NldCkpXjIpXG59XG5tc2VcbmBgYCJ9 -->

```r
set.seed(3)
train <- sample(n, n / 2)
validation_set <- df[-train,]
degree_max <- 5
mse <- rep(0, times = degree_max)
for (i in 1:degree_max) {
  df_lm <- lm(SalePrice ~ poly(Overall.Qual, degree = i), data = df, subset = train)
  mse[i] <- mean((validation_set$SalePrice - predict(df_lm, validation_set))^2)
}
mse
```

<!-- rnb-source-end -->

<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxubGlicmFyeShib290KVxuZGVncmVlX21heCA8LSA1XG5jb21wdXRlX2xvb2N2X21zZSA8LSBmdW5jdGlvbihkZWdyZWUpIHtcbiAgZGZfZ2xtIDwtIGdsbShTYWxlUHJpY2UgfiBwb2x5KE92ZXJhbGwuUXVhbCwgZGVncmVlKSwgZGF0YSA9IGRmKVxuICBjdi5nbG0oZGYsIGRmX2dsbSkkZGVsdGFbMV1cbn1cbm1zZSA8LSB2YXBwbHkoMTpkZWdyZWVfbWF4LCBjb21wdXRlX2xvb2N2X21zZSwgRlVOLlZBTFVFID0gbnVtZXJpYygxKSlcbm1zZVxuYGBgIn0= -->

```r
library(boot)
degree_max <- 5
compute_loocv_mse <- function(degree) {
  df_glm <- glm(SalePrice ~ poly(Overall.Qual, degree), data = df)
  cv.glm(df, df_glm)$delta[1]
}
mse <- vapply(1:degree_max, compute_loocv_mse, FUN.VALUE = numeric(1))
mse
```

<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxuXG5jb21wdXRlX2tjdl9tc2UgPC0gZnVuY3Rpb24oZGVncmVlLCBrKSB7XG4gIGRmX2dsbSA8LSBnbG0oU2FsZVByaWNlIH4gcG9seShPdmVyYWxsLlF1YWwsIGRlZ3JlZSksIGRhdGEgPSBkZilcbiAgY3YuZ2xtKGRmLCBkZl9nbG0sIEsgPSBrKSRkZWx0YVsxXVxufVxubXNlIDwtIHZhcHBseSgxOmRlZ3JlZV9tYXgsIGNvbXB1dGVfa2N2X21zZSwgayA9IDEwLCBGVU4uVkFMVUUgPSBudW1lcmljKDEpKVxubXNlXG5gYGAifQ== -->

```r

compute_kcv_mse <- function(degree, k) {
  df_glm <- glm(SalePrice ~ poly(Overall.Qual, degree), data = df)
  cv.glm(df, df_glm, K = k)$delta[1]
}
mse <- vapply(1:degree_max, compute_kcv_mse, k = 10, FUN.VALUE = numeric(1))
mse
```

```r
lm_coefs <- function(data, index = 1:nrow(data)) {
  coef(lm(SalePrice ~ Overall.Qual, data = df, subset = index))
}
```
